4206/*-



4207 * The generated code includes comments that allow you to trace directly



4208 * back to the appropriate location in the model.  The basic format



4209 * is <system>/block_name, where system is the system number (uniquely



4210 * assigned by Simulink) and block_name is the name of the block.



4211 *



4212 * Use the MATLAB hilite_system command to trace the generated code back



4213 * to the model.  For example,



4214 *



4215 * hilite_system('<S3>')    - opens system 3



4216 * hilite_system('<S3>/Kp') - opens and selects block Kp which resides in S3



4217 *

4219 *
